
</ul>
</div>

<th colspan="10" style="font-size: 0.85em; font-weight: normal; text-align: left; padding: 4px"><b>Notes</b>:<br />
<dl><dd><span class="citation wikicite" id="endnote_post-fukushima-shutdown"><b><a href="#ref_post-fukushima-shutdown">^a</a></b></span>  <i>Post-Fukushima shutdown of eight reactors.</i> On 15 March 2011, the <a href="/wiki/German_Government" class="mw-redirect" title="German Government">German Government</a> decided to close seven nuclear power plants built before 1980 along with the <i>Krümmel nuclear power plant</i> for a duration of three months.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> The temporary shutdown was changed into permanent shutdown by the German parliament on 30 June 2012. The remaining nine plants that stayed operational were given new decommissioning dates.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></dd></dl>
</th></tr></tbody></table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">United States</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_commercial_nuclear_reactors&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: United States">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_cancelled_nuclear_reactors_in_the_United_States" title="List of cancelled nuclear reactors in the United States">List of cancelled nuclear reactors in the United States</a>, <a href="/wiki/Army_Nuclear_Power_Program" title="Army Nuclear Power Program">Army Nuclear Power Program</a>, and <a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Naval_reactors" title="List of United States Naval reactors">List of United States Naval reactors</a></div>
